V_R0010_OUTSTANDBAL := 
    V_R0020_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0030_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0040_OUTSTANDBAL +
    V_R0050_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0060_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0070_OUTSTANDBAL +
    V_R0080_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0090_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0100_OUTSTANDBAL +
    V_R0110_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0120_OUTSTANDBAL;

V_R0010_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL := 
    V_R0020_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0030_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0040_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL +
    V_R0050_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0060_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0070_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL +
    V_R0080_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0090_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL + V_R0100_SECURED_OUTSTANDBAL +
